toggle_county_trade = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_county_trade
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_county_trade
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_fiber
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_metal
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_tools
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_county_trade
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_food
				value = county.var:trade_price_food
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_cereal
				value = county.var:trade_price_cereal
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_salted
				value = county.var:trade_price_salted
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_salt
				value = county.var:trade_price_salt
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_mud
				value = county.var:trade_price_mud
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_fuel
				value = county.var:trade_price_fuel
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_fiber
				value = county.var:trade_price_fiber
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_timber
				value = county.var:trade_price_timber
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_metal
				value = county.var:trade_price_metal
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_exotics_w
				value = county.var:trade_price_exotics_w
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_exotics_e
				value = county.var:trade_price_exotics_e
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_exotics_g
				value = county.var:trade_price_exotics_g
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_textile
				value = county.var:trade_price_textile
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_pottery
				value = county.var:trade_price_pottery
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_county_price_tools
				value = county.var:trade_price_tools
			}
		}
	}
}
close_county_trade = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_county_trade
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_county_trade
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_fiber
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_metal
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_county_price_tools
		}
	}
}

	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes

	is_valid = { 
		always = yes

	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_prov_trade
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_prov_trade
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_food
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_cereal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_salted
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_salt
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_mud
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_fuel
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_fiber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_fiber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_fiber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_fiber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_fiber

			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_fiber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_fiber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_timber
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_metal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_metal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_metal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_metal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_metal

			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_metal

			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_metal
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_exotics_w
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_exotics_e
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_exotics_g
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_textile
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_pottery
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_sply_tools
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_tools
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_tools
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_tools
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_tools
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_tools
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_pop_tools
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_prod_tools
			remove_variable = info_trade_prov_in_build_tools
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_prov_trade
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_sply_food
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_food
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_food
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_food
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_food
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_food
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_food
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_prod_food
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_build_food
				value = 0
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_calorie_food
					var:pop_calorie_food > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_food
					add = var:pop_calorie_food
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_calorie_actual_food
					var:pop_calorie_actual_food > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_food
					add = var:pop_calorie_actual_food
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_nutrient_food
					var:pop_nutrient_food > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_food
					add = var:pop_nutrient_food
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_nutrient_actual_food
					var:pop_nutrient_actual_food > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_food
					add = var:pop_nutrient_actual_food
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_comfort_food
					var:pop_comfort_food > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_food
					add = var:pop_comfort_food
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_comfort_actual_food
					var:pop_comfort_actual_food > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_food
					add = var:pop_comfort_actual_food
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_luxury_food
					var:pop_luxury_food > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_food
					add = var:pop_luxury_food
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_luxury_actual_food
					var:pop_luxury_actual_food > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_food
					add = var:pop_luxury_actual_food
				}
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = prod_instances
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = prod_sply_old_food
						var:prod_sply_old_food > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = info_trade_prov_sply_food
							add = prev.var:prod_sply_old_food
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = prod_dmnd_old_food
						var:prod_dmnd_old_food > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_food
							add = prev.var:prod_dmnd_old_food
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = prod_in_old_food
						var:prod_in_old_food > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = info_trade_prov_in_prod_food
							add = prev.var:prod_in_old_food
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = build_slots
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = build_food
						var:build_food > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_food
							add = prev.var:build_food
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = build_in_food
						var:build_in_food > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = info_trade_prov_in_build_food
							add = prev.var:build_in_food
						}
					}
				}
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_food
				add = var:info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_food
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_food
				add = var:info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_food
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_food
				add = var:info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_food
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_food
				add = var:info_trade_prov_in_pop_food
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_food
				add = var:info_trade_prov_in_prod_food
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_food
				add = var:info_trade_prov_in_build_food
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_sply_cereal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_cereal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_cereal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_cereal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_cereal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_cereal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_cereal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_prod_cereal
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_trade_prov_in_build_cereal
				value = 0
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_calorie_cereal
					var:pop_calorie_cereal > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_cereal
					add = var:pop_calorie_cereal
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_calorie_actual_cereal
					var:pop_calorie_actual_cereal > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_cereal
					add = var:pop_calorie_actual_cereal
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_nutrient_cereal
					var:pop_nutrient_cereal > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_cereal
					add = var:pop_nutrient_cereal
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_nutrient_actual_cereal
					var:pop_nutrient_actual_cereal > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_cereal
					add = var:pop_nutrient_actual_cereal
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_comfort_cereal
					var:pop_comfort_cereal > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_cereal
					add = var:pop_comfort_cereal
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_comfort_actual_cereal
					var:pop_comfort_actual_cereal > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_cereal
					add = var:pop_comfort_actual_cereal
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_luxury_cereal
					var:pop_luxury_cereal > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_pop_cereal
					add = var:pop_luxury_cereal
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					has_variable = pop_luxury_actual_cereal
					var:pop_luxury_actual_cereal > 0
				}
				change_variable = { 
					name = info_trade_prov_in_pop_cereal
					add = var:pop_luxury_actual_cereal
				}
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = prod_instances
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = prod_sply_old_cereal
						var:prod_sply_old_cereal > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = info_trade_prov_sply_cereal
							add = prev.var:prod_sply_old_cereal
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = prod_dmnd_old_cereal
						var:prod_dmnd_old_cereal > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_prod_cereal
							add = prev.var:prod_dmnd_old_cereal
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = prod_in_old_cereal
						var:prod_in_old_cereal > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = info_trade_prov_in_prod_cereal
							add = prev.var:prod_in_old_cereal
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = build_slots
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						has_variable = build_cereal
						var:build_cereal > 0
					}
					prev = { 
						change_variable = { 
							name = info_trade_prov_dmnd_build_cereal
							add = prev.var:build_cereal
						}
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = {

				}
			}
			every_in_list = {

toggle_prov_pop = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_prov_pop
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_prov_pop
			remove_variable = info_pop_prov_earn_pop
			remove_variable = info_pop_prov_pay_pop
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_farm
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_farm
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_workshop
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_workshop
				value = 0
			}
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_prov_pop
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pop
				value = var:pop_earn_free
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pop
				add = var:pop_earn_serf
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pop
				value = var:pop_pay_free
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pop
				add = var:pop_pay_serf
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { 
						has_variable = extraction_potential
					}
				}
				set_variable = { 
					name = extraction_potential
					value = 0
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_farm
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_farm
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_farm
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_farm
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_farm
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_pasture
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_pasture
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_pasture
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_forest
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_forest
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_forest
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_forest
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_extraction
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_extraction
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_extraction
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_workshop
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_workshop
				value = 0
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				limit = { 
					var:prod_template = { 
						has_variable = prod_land_workshop
					}
				}
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_earn_workshop
						add = prev.var:prod_earn
					}
					change_variable = { 
						name = info_pop_prov_pay_workshop
						add = prev.var:prod_pay_old
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
close_prov_pop = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_prov_pop
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_prov_pop
			remove_variable = info_pop_prov_earn_pop
			remove_variable = info_pop_prov_pay_pop
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_farm
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_farm
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_pasture
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_forest
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_extraction
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_earn_workshop
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_pop_prov_pay_workshop
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = toggled_prov_prod
			}
			remove_variable = toggled_prov_prod
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_prov_prod
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_val_2_pottery

			remove_variable = info_dat_county_out_val_2_tools

			remove_variable = info_dat_county_in_val_2_tools

			limit = { 
				has_variable = trade_county
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = toggled_county_dat
				value = 1
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = trade_dat_food
				prev = { 
					add_to_variable_list = { 
						name = toggled_county_dat_t
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = array_trade_dat_food
				prev = { 
					add_to_variable_list = { 
						name = array_toggled_county_dat_t
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_t
				value = 0
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_tt
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_t
				value = -210000
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = array_toggled_county_dat_t
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						prev.var:array_get_max_t = { 
							compare_value < prev
						}
					}
					set_global_variable = { 
						name = array_get_max_tt
						value = global_var:array_get_max_t
					}
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_t
							value = prev
						}
					}
				}
				change_global_variable = { 
					name = array_get_max_t
					add = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_dat_county_out_val_0_food
				value = var:array_get_max_t
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_dat_county_out_val_0_food
				divide = 100
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = toggled_county_dat_t
				value = global_var:array_get_max_tt
			}
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_t
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_tt
			remove_variable = array_get_max_t
			ordered_in_list = { 
				variable = toggled_county_dat_t
				position = global_var:toggled_county_dat_t.compare_value
				prev = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = info_dat_county_out_scope_0_food
						value = prev.var:trade_location
					}
					remove_list_variable = { 
						name = toggled_county_dat_t
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_list = { 
				variable = array_toggled_county_dat_t
				position = global_var:toggled_county_dat_t.compare_value
				prev = { 
					remove_list_variable = { 
						name = array_toggled_county_dat_t
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_t
				value = 0
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_tt
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = array_get_max_t
				value = -210000
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = array_toggled_county_dat_t
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						prev.var:array_get_max_t = { 
							compare_value < prev
						}
					}
					set_global_variable = { 
						name = array_get_max_tt
						value = global_var:array_get_max_t
					}
					prev = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = array_get_max_t
							value = prev
						}
					}
				}
				change_global_variable = { 
					name = array_get_max_t
					add = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = info_dat_county_out_val_1_food
				value = var:array_get_max_t
			}
			change_variable = { 
				name = info_dat_county_out_val_1_food
				divide = 100
			}
			set_global_variable = { 
				name = toggled_county_dat_t
				value = global_var:array_get_max_tt
			}
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_t
			remove_global_variable = array_get_max_tt
			remove_variable = array_get_max_t
			ordered_in_list = { 
				variable = toggled_county_dat_t
				position = global_var:toggled_county_dat_t.compare_value
				prev = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = info_dat_county_out_scope_1_food
						value = prev.var:trade_location
					}
					remove_list_variable = { 
						name = toggled_county_dat_t
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_list = { 
				variable = array_toggled_county_dat_t
				position = global_var:toggled_county_dat_t.compare_value

						name = info_dat_county_in_scope_2_tools
						value = prev.var:trade_location
					}
					remove_list_variable = { 
						name = toggled_county_dat_t
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_list = { 
				variable = array_toggled_county_dat_t
				position = global_var:toggled_county_dat_t.compare_value
				prev = { 
					remove_list_variable = { 
						name = array_toggled_county_dat_t
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			remove_global_variable = toggled_county_dat_t
			remove_variable = toggled_county_dat_t
		}
	}
}
